SELECT [t].[UserId], [t].[AvatarUrl], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[Email], [t].[FullName], [t].[IsActive], [t].[IsEmailVerified], [t].[LastLoginAt], [t].[PasswordHash], [t].[PhoneNumber], [t].[RoleId], [t].[SchoolId], [t].[UpdatedAt], [t].[RoleId0], [t].[Description], [t].[RoleCode], [t].[RoleName], [s].[ProfileId], [s].[AdmissionDate], [s].[AdmissionType], [s].[DateOfBirth], [s].[EthnicGroup], [s].[Gender], [s].[PermanentAddress], [s].[PlaceOfBirth], [s].[SchoolId], [s].[StudentCode], [s].[UserId], [t0].[ProfileId], [t0].[BankAccountNumber], [t0].[BankName], [t0].[ContractType], [t0].[DateOfBirth], [t0].[Gender], [t0].[HireDate], [t0].[Qualification], [t0].[SchoolId], [t0].[SpecializationSubject], [t0].[TaxCode], [t0].[TeacherCode], [t0].[UserId], [s0].[ProfileId], [s0].[DateOfBirth], [s0].[Gender], [s0].[HireDate], [s0].[SchoolId], [s0].[SupervisorCode], [s0].[UserId], [p].[ProfileId], [p].[Occupation], [p].[SchoolId], [p].[UserId], [p].[WorkAddress]
FROM (
    SELECT [u].[UserId], [u].[AvatarUrl], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[Email], [u].[FullName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsEmailVerified], [u].[LastLoginAt], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[RoleId], [u].[SchoolId], [u].[UpdatedAt], [r].[RoleId] AS [RoleId0], [r].[Description], [r].[RoleCode], [r].[RoleName]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[RoleId]
    WHERE [u].[SchoolId] = @__schoolId_0 AND [r].[RoleCode] = @__ToUpper_1 AND [r].[RoleCode] IN (N'STUDENT', N'TEACHER', N'SUPERVISOR', N'PARENT')
    ORDER BY [u].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_2 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_3 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
